48:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":"You know what? Functions delivering to LLM must have only one parameter of object type. 49:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["Also, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@agentica"}]," does not allow a function of returning an union type with ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"undefined"}],".
